			limit = {
				NOT = {
					RAJ = {
						has_idea = idea_raj_chauth_1
					}
					RAJ = {
						has_idea = idea_raj_chauth_2
					}
					RAJ = {
						has_idea = idea_raj_chauth_3
					}
					RAJ = {
						has_idea = idea_raj_chauth_4
					}
					RAJ = {
						has_idea = idea_raj_chauth_5
					}
				}
			}
			RAJ = {
				add_ideas = idea_raj_chauth_1
			}
			RAJ = {
				country_event = {
					hours = 5
					id = india.704
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RAJ = {
					has_idea = idea_raj_chauth_1
				}
			}
			RAJ = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = idea_raj_chauth_1
					add_idea = idea_raj_chauth_2
				}
			}
			RAJ = {

				}
			}
		}

				RAJ = {

				}
			}

#panag declares socialist state#
country_event = {
	id = india.914
	title = india.914.t
	desc = india.914.d
	picture = india_panag_pui
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		#glory to the new socialist order# People's Union of Indian  Republics#
		name = india.914.o1
		hidden_effect = {
			PUI = {
				country_event = {
					days = 3
					id = pui.1
				}
			}
			PUI = {
				annex_country = {
					target = RAJ
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
			PUI = {
				change_tag_from = RAJ
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			RAJ = {
				PUI = {
					transfer_technology = yes
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = RAJ
				}
				add_core_of = PUI
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		##panag has gone too far#
		name = india.914.o2
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Harcharanjit Singh Panag"
			picture = "Portrait_RAJ_Harcharanjit_Singh_Panag.dds"
			ideology = revolutionary_socialist_ideology
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = revolutionary_socialist
			long_name = RAJ_panag_uprising_long
			name = RAJ_panag_uprising
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "H.D.Deve Gowda"
			picture = "Portrait_RAJ_Deve_Gowda.dds"
			ideology = centrist_ideology
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = centrist
			long_name = RAJ_new_janata_party
			name = RAJ_new_janata_party
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = revolutionary_socialist
			size = 0.5
		}
		set_country_flag = flag_raj_civil_war
		set_country_flag = flag_raj_can_elect_janata
	}
}

#INC splits liberal-new_democrat# 
country_event = {
	id = india.917
	title = india.917.t
	desc = india.917.d
	picture = india_inc_split
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = india.917.o1
		set_country_flag = flag_raj_inc_liberal
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = india_singh_pm
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Manmohan Singh"
				picture = "Portrait_RAJ_Manmohan_Singh.dds"
				ideology = social_liberal
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = flag_raj_inc_mukherjee
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Pranab Mukherjee"
				picture = "Portrait_RAJ_Pranab_Mukherjee.dds"
				ideology = social_liberal
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = flag_raj_inc_rahul
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Rahul Gandhi"
				picture = "Portrait_RAJ_Rahul_Gandhi.dds"
				ideology = social_liberal
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = flag_raj_inc_pawar
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Sharad Pawar"
				picture = "Portrait_RAJ_Sharad_Pawar.dds"
				ideology = social_liberal
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = india_singh_pm
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = flag_raj_inc_mukherjee
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = flag_raj_inc_rahul
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = flag_raj_inc_pawar
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Rajiv Gandhi"
				picture = "Portrait_RAJ_Rajiv_Ghandi.dds"
				ideology = social_liberal
			}
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Mamata Banerjee"
			picture = "Portrait_RAJ_Mamata_Banerjee.dds"
			ideology = new_democrat_ideology
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = new_democrat
			long_name = RAJ_inc_t_long
			name = RAJ_inc_t
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = liberal
			long_name = RAJ_inc_lib_long
			name = RAJ_inc_lib
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = liberal
			popularity = 0.3
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = new_democrat
			popularity = -0.4
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = new_democrat
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = liberal
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
	}
}

#2012 General Election
country_event = {
	id = india.918
	title = india.918.t
	desc = india.918.d
	picture = india_elections
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = RAJ
		date > 2012.1.10
		date < 2012.1.20
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = india_emergency
		}
		OR = {
			has_government = national_conservative
			has_government = centrist
			has_government = liberal
			has_government = new_democrat
			has_government = moderate_socialist
		}
	}
	option = {
		#INC #
		name = india.918.o1
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = RAJ_rss_extreme
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = flag_raj_inc_liberal
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = liberal
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			else = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = new_democrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
		}
	}
	option = {
		#BJS
		name = india.918.o2
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = national_conservative
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}
	option = {
		#Left Front#
		name = india.918.o3
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = RAJ_rss_extreme
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

				name = "Ardhendu Bhusan Bardhan"
				picture = "Portrait_RAJ_Ardhendu_Bhusan_Bardhan.dds"
				ideology = democratic_socialist
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = flag_raj_left_front_chatterjee
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Somnath Chatterjee"
				picture = "Portrait_RAJ_Somnath_Chatterjee.dds"
				ideology = democratic_socialist
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = flag_raj_left_front_karat
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Prakash Karat"
				picture = "Portrait_RAJ_Prakash_Karat.dds"
				ideology = democratic_socialist
			}
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = moderate_socialist
			long_name = RAJ_left_front_long
			name = RAJ_left_front
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = moderate_socialist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
	}
	option = {
		#emergency#
		name = india.918.o6
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}

#post civil-war reclaimation?#
country_event = {
	id = india.923
	title = india.923.t
	desc = india.923.d
	picture = india_post_civil_war
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = RAJ
			tag = RAJ
		}
		has_country_flag = flag_raj_civil_war
		has_civil_war = no
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 12
	}
	option = {
		#reclaim seceders#
		name = india.923.o1
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = KAS
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = KAS
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = KHA
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = KHA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = NGA
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = NGA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = MNP
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = MNP
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = MZO
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = MZO
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = flag_raj_civil_war
	}
	option = {
		#status quo#
		name = india.923.o2
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		add_political_power = -200
		clr_country_flag = flag_raj_civil_war
	}
}

#Kashmir secedes#
country_event = {
	id = india.924
	title = india.924.t
	desc = india.924.d
	picture = india_dem_for_kashmir_revolt
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = RAJ
		RAJ = {
			controls_state = 441
		}
		NOT = {
			RAJ = {
				has_completed_focus = RAJ_kashmir_india_peace
			}
		}
		has_civil_war = yes
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 15
	}
	option = {
		#let go#
		name = india.924.o1
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		release = KAS
		KAS = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = moderate_socialist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		KAS = {
			transfer_state = 441
		}
		KAS = {
			load_oob = generic_2000
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			PAK = {
				country_event = {
					days = 1
					id = india.926
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#crush#
		name = india.924.o2
		KAS = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = moderate_socialist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = RAJ
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = KAS
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		release = KAS
		KAS = {
			transfer_state = 441
		}
		KAS = {
			load_oob = generic_2000
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = KAS
			type = annex_everything
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			PAK = {
				country_event = {
					days = 1
					id = india.925
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		#y#

			factor = 75
		}
		RAJ = {
			country_event = {
				hours = 10
				id = india.932
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			hours = 5
			id = india.933
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Shangwang Shangyung Khaplang"
			picture = "Portrait_NGA_Shangwang_Shangyung_Khaplang.dds"
			ideology = national_bolshevik_ideology
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = national_bolshevik
			long_name = NGA_nscn_k_long
			name = NGA_nscn_k
		}
	}
	option = {
		#n#
		name = india.931.o2
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
				}
				50 = {
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Shangwang Shangyung Khaplang"
						picture = "Portrait_NGA_Shangwang_Shangyung_Khaplang.dds"

						ideology = fascist
						long_name = NGA_nscn_k_long

#Manipur secedes following threat from nagalim and mizoram seccession#

	id = india.938

	desc = india.938.d
	picture = india_civwar_manipur

		tag = RAJ
		RAJ = {
			controls_state = 957
		}
		has_civil_war = yes
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 80
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		#let go#
		name = india.938.o1
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		release = MNP
		MNP = {
			transfer_state = 957
		}
		MNP = {
			load_oob = MNP_2000
		}
		MNP = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = national_conservative
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
				}
				50 = {
					country_event = {
						days = 5
						id = india.939
					}
					MNP = {
						country_event = {
							days = 5
							id = india.939
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#crush#
		name = india.938.o2
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = RAJ
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = MNP
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		release = MNP
		MNP = {
			transfer_state = 957
		}
		MNP = {
			load_oob = MNP_2000
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = MNP
			type = annex_everything
		}
		MNP = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = national_conservative
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				40 = {
				}
				60 = {
					country_event = {
						days = 5
						id = india.939
					}
					MNP = {
						country_event = {
							days = 5
							id = india.939
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
